# TumioParbe Frontend Debug Info

## Last Update: [Date: ${new Date().toISOString()}]

### API Response Debug
This file captures API response data to help debug issues in the application.

### Issue: Empty Courses Page
The courses page shows no data despite API calls completing successfully.

Debug output:
- Fetching students...
- Fetching enrollments...
- Fetching courses...
- Found 0 students
- Found 0 courses 
- Found 0 enrollments

### Possible Causes:
1. API returning empty arrays instead of expected data
2. Data structure mismatch (e.g., API returning { results: [] } but code accessing .data directly)
3. Empty response data due to authentication issues
4. Incorrect API endpoints or parameters
5. Data processing errors in the frontend

### Next Steps:
1. Add detailed API response logging to the courses page
2. Check the actual response format from each API endpoint
3. Verify authentication tokens are valid
4. Compare expected vs actual data structures
